Express Pay Payout Documentation
Required Request Headers
Every API request must include the following mandatory headers for authentication and identification:

Header Name	Value (Example)	Description
partnerid	2400xx	Unique Partner / Merchant identifier provided by us.
consumerkey	21b9c1f6195fxxxx	API consumer key used for request authentication.
consumersecret	ecdad1614bd1xxxx	API consumer secret used to validate and secure API requests.

POST bankList

https://api.sparkuptech.in/api/fzep/payout/bankList

HEADERS
partnerid 2400xx

consumerkey 21b9c1f6195fxxxx

consumersecret ecdad1614bd1xxxx

Example Request
curl --location --request POST 'https://api.sparkuptech.in/api/fzep/payout/bankList' \
--header 'partnerid: 2400xx' \
--header 'consumerkey: 21b9c1f6195fxxxx' \
--header 'consumersecret: ecdad1614bd1xxxx'

POST expressPay

https://api.sparkuptech.in/api/fzep/payout/expressPay2

HEADERS
partnerid 2400xx

consumerkey 21b9c1f6195fxxxx

consumersecret ecdad1614bd1xxxx

Body
raw (json)

{
  "AccountNo": "1234567890",
  "AmountR": 1500,
  "APIRequestID": 9876543210123456,
  "BankID": 1105,
  "BeneMobile": "9876543210",
  "BeneName": "John Doe",
  "bankName": "HDFC BANK",
  "IFSC": "HDFC0001234",
  "SenderEmail": "demouser@example.com",
  "SenderMobile": "9123456789",
  "SenderName": "sender name",
  "paymentType": "IMPS",
  "WebHook": "https://yourdomain.com/webhook",
  "extraParam1": "NA",
  "extraParam2": "NA",
  "extraField1": "TestValue",
  "sub_service_name": "ExpressPay",
  "remark": "Test Transaction"
}


Example Request

curl --location 'https://api.sparkuptech.in/api/fzep/payout/expressPay2' \
--header 'partnerid: 2400xx' \
--header 'consumerkey: 21b9c1f6195fxxxx' \
--header 'consumersecret: ecdad1614bd1xxxx' \
--data-raw '{
  "AccountNo": "1234567890",
  "AmountR": 1500,
  "APIRequestID": 9876543210123456,
  "BankID": 1105,
  "BeneMobile": "9876543210",
  "BeneName": "John Doe",
  "bankName": "HDFC BANK",
  "IFSC": "HDFC0001234",
  "SenderEmail": "demouser@example.com",
  "SenderMobile": "9123456789",
  "SenderName": "sender name",
  "paymentType": "IMPS",
  "WebHook": "https://yourdomain.com/webhook",
  "extraParam1": "NA",
  "extraParam2": "NA",
  "extraField1": "TestValue",
  "sub_service_name": "ExpressPay",
  "remark": "Test Transaction"
}
'

Example Response
Body

{
  "success": true,
  "message": "Transaction is under pending....",
  "data": {
    "clientReqId": 7073592984484542,
    "totalAmount": 1500,
    "serviceCharge": 0,
    "transactionAmount": 1500,
    "referenceNo": null,
    "transaction_id": "UTR1215432465753",
    "status": "pending",
    "remark": "Amount of 1500 is pending",
    "paymentType": "IMPS"
  }
}
